<span id="cb2-14"><a href="#cb2-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">ggplot</span>(<span class="fu">aes</span>(<span class="at">x=</span>year, <span class="at">y=</span>n, <span class="at">fill=</span>query)) <span class="sc">+</span></span>
<span id="cb2-15"><a href="#cb2-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">geom_point</span>(<span class="fu">aes</span>(<span class="at">shape=</span>query), <span class="at">size =</span> <span class="fl">1.5</span>) <span class="sc">+</span></span>
<span id="cb2-16"><a href="#cb2-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">geom_line</span>(<span class="fu">aes</span>(<span class="at">linetype=</span>query)) <span class="sc">+</span></span>
<span id="cb2-17"><a href="#cb2-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">theme_minimal</span>() <span class="sc">+</span></span>
<span id="cb2-18"><a href="#cb2-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">xlab</span>(<span class="st">"Year"</span>) <span class="sc">+</span></span>
<span id="cb2-19"><a href="#cb2-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">ylab</span>(<span class="st">"Number of Publications"</span>) <span class="sc">+</span></span>
<span id="cb2-20"><a href="#cb2-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">theme</span>(<span class="at">legend.position=</span><span class="st">"bottom"</span>) <span class="sc">+</span></span>
<span id="cb2-21"><a href="#cb2-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">guides</span>(<span class="at">fill=</span><span class="fu">guide_legend</span>(<span class="at">title=</span><span class="st">"Search Query:"</span>),</span>
<span id="cb2-22"><a href="#cb2-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>         <span class="at">shape=</span><span class="fu">guide_legend</span>(<span class="at">title=</span><span class="st">"Search Query:"</span>),</span>
<span id="cb2-23"><a href="#cb2-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>         <span class="at">linetype=</span><span class="fu">guide_legend</span>(<span class="at">title=</span><span class="st">"Search Query:"</span>))</span>
<span id="cb2-24"><a href="#cb2-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb2-25"><a href="#cb2-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>scopus_grph <span class="sc">+</span> <span class="fu">annotation_custom</span>(<span class="fu">ggplotGrob</span>(graph_table),</span>
<span id="cb2-26"><a href="#cb2-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                              <span class="at">xmin =</span> <span class="fl">2002.5</span>, <span class="at">ymin =</span> <span class="dv">8100</span>,</span>
<span id="cb2-27"><a href="#cb2-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                              <span class="at">xmax =</span> <span class="fl">2007.5</span>)</span></code><button title="Copy to Clipboard" class="code-copy-button"><i class="bi"></i></button></pre></div>
</details>
<div class="cell-output-display">
<div class="quarto-figure quarto-figure-center">
<figure class="figure">
<p><img src="analysis_files/figure-html/scopus-analysis-1-1.png" class="img-fluid figure-img" width="672"></p>
<p></p><figcaption class="figure-caption">Publications listed on Scopus between 2001-2021.</figcaption><p></p>
</figure>

</div>
<details>
<summary>Code</summary>
<div class="sourceCode cell-code" id="cb3"><pre class="sourceCode r code-with-copy"><code class="sourceCode r"><span id="cb3-1"><a href="#cb3-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># Saving Figure</span></span>
<span id="cb3-2"><a href="#cb3-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">ggsave</span>(<span class="st">"scopus_1.pdf"</span>, <span class="at">path =</span> <span class="fu">file.path</span>(<span class="fu">getwd</span>(), <span class="st">"figs"</span>), <span class="at">device=</span><span class="st">"pdf"</span>, <span class="at">dpi=</span><span class="dv">800</span>)</span></code><button title="Copy to Clipboard" class="code-copy-button"><i class="bi"></i></button></pre></div>
</details>
</div>
<p><strong>Query Method:</strong> For the query of the subject fields, terms were searched for within the titles, abstracts, and keywords of publications listed on Scopus. For the query related to Computational Text Analysis in social sciences (CTA in SOCI) and Radicalism, the search was limited to the Scopus subject category ‚Äúsocial sciences‚Äù. This is also due to the fact that terms related to the root word ‚Äúradical‚Äù often have a different meaning in the natural sciences. For the search query related to CTA, related domains (e.g.&nbsp;Quantitative Text Analysis and Natural Language Processing), as well as common methods also searched for.</p>
<p>Search Terms:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>Computational Text Analysis (CTA): ((TITLE-ABS-KEY (‚Äúquantitative text‚Äù OR ‚Äúcomputational text‚Äù OR ‚Äúnatural language processing‚Äù OR ‚Äúquantitative content analysis‚Äù OR ‚Äúquantitative content analyses‚Äù) OR TITLE-ABS-KEY(‚Äúsentiment analysis‚Äù OR ‚Äúsentiment analyses‚Äù OR ‚Äúnamed entity recognition‚Äù OR ‚Äútopic model‚Äù OR ‚Äútopic modeling‚Äù OR ‚Äútopic models‚Äù) OR TITLE-ABS-KEY(‚Äútext classification‚Äù OR ‚Äúkey word extraction‚Äù OR ‚Äúlemmatization‚Äù OR ‚Äúword embedding‚Äù)))</p></li>
<li><p>Computational Text Analysis in Social Sciences (CTA IN SOCI): CTA AND ( LIMIT-TO ( SUBJAREA,‚ÄúSOCI‚Äù ) ) )</p></li>
<li><p>Radicalism: ((TITLE-ABS-KEY (radicali OR terrorist OR terrorism OR ‚Äúpolitical violence‚Äù OR extremi OR ‚Äúfar left‚Äù OR ‚Äúfar right‚Äù OR islamist OR islamism OR fundamentalis OR jihad) ) AND ( LIMIT-TO ( SUBJAREA,‚ÄúSOCI‚Äù ) ) )</p></li>
<li><p>CTA+Radicalism: Intersection of the CTA and Radicalism query</p></li>
</ul>
</section>

<span id="cb8-31"><a href="#cb8-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>         <span class="at">remove_url =</span> T, </span>

<span id="cb8-34"><a href="#cb8-34" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">tokens_remove</span>(<span class="fu">stopwords</span>(<span class="st">"english"</span>, <span class="at">source =</span> <span class="st">"marimo"</span>)) <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>

<section id="exploring-content-topic-modeling" class="level2">
<h2 class="anchored" data-anchor-id="exploring-content-topic-modeling">Exploring Content: Topic Modeling</h2>
<div class="cell">
<details>
<summary>Code</summary>
<div class="sourceCode cell-code" id="cb20"><pre class="sourceCode r code-with-copy"><code class="sourceCode r"><span id="cb20-1"><a href="#cb20-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># Creating Figure</span></span>
<span id="cb20-2"><a href="#cb20-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>dfm_post.new <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">dfm_subset</span>(dfm_post, <span class="fu">ntoken</span>(dfm_post) <span class="sc">&gt;</span> <span class="dv">0</span>)</span>
<span id="cb20-3"><a href="#cb20-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-4"><a href="#cb20-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>result <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">FindTopicsNumber</span>(</span>
<span id="cb20-5"><a href="#cb20-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  dfm_post.new,</span>
<span id="cb20-6"><a href="#cb20-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">topics =</span> <span class="fu">seq</span>(<span class="at">from =</span> <span class="dv">2</span>, <span class="at">to =</span> <span class="dv">50</span>, <span class="at">by =</span> <span class="dv">1</span>),</span>
<span id="cb20-7"><a href="#cb20-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">metrics =</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="st">"Griffiths2004"</span>, <span class="st">"CaoJuan2009"</span>, <span class="st">"Arun2010"</span>, <span class="st">"Deveaud2014"</span>),</span>
<span id="cb20-8"><a href="#cb20-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">method =</span> <span class="st">"Gibbs"</span>,</span>
<span id="cb20-9"><a href="#cb20-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">control =</span> <span class="fu">list</span>(<span class="at">seed =</span><span class="dv">1234</span>),</span>
<span id="cb20-10"><a href="#cb20-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">mc.cores =</span> <span class="cn">NA</span>,</span>
<span id="cb20-11"><a href="#cb20-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">verbose =</span> <span class="cn">FALSE</span>)</span>
<span id="cb20-12"><a href="#cb20-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb20-13"><a href="#cb20-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># Create function to plot figure</span></span>
<span id="cb20-14"><a href="#cb20-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>lda_plot <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="cf">function</span> (values)</span>
<span id="cb20-15"><a href="#cb20-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>{</span>
<span id="cb20-16"><a href="#cb20-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="cf">if</span> (<span class="st">"LDA_model"</span> <span class="sc">%in%</span> <span class="fu">names</span>(values)) {</span>
<span id="cb20-17"><a href="#cb20-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    values <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> values[<span class="sc">!</span><span class="fu">names</span>(values) <span class="sc">%in%</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="st">"LDA_model"</span>)]</span>
<span id="cb20-18"><a href="#cb20-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb20-19"><a href="#cb20-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  columns <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> base<span class="sc">::</span><span class="fu">subset</span>(values, <span class="at">select =</span> <span class="dv">2</span><span class="sc">:</span><span class="fu">ncol</span>(values))</span>
<span id="cb20-20"><a href="#cb20-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  values <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> base<span class="sc">::</span><span class="fu">data.frame</span>(values[<span class="st">"topics"</span>], base<span class="sc">::</span><span class="fu">apply</span>(columns,</span>
<span id="cb20-21"><a href="#cb20-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                                           <span class="dv">2</span>, <span class="cf">function</span>(column) {</span>
<span id="cb20-22"><a href="#cb20-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                                             scales<span class="sc">::</span><span class="fu">rescale</span>(column, <span class="at">to =</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="dv">0</span>, <span class="dv">1</span>), <span class="at">from =</span> <span class="fu">range</span>(column))</span>
<span id="cb20-23"><a href="#cb20-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                                           }))</span>
<span id="cb20-24"><a href="#cb20-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  values <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> reshape2<span class="sc">::</span><span class="fu">melt</span>(values, <span class="at">id.vars =</span> <span class="st">"topics"</span>,</span>
<span id="cb20-25"><a href="#cb20-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                           <span class="at">na.rm =</span> <span class="cn">TRUE</span>)</span>
<span id="cb20-26"><a href="#cb20-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  values<span class="sc">$</span>group <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> values<span class="sc">$</span>variable <span class="sc">%in%</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="st">"Griffiths2004"</span>,</span>
<span id="cb20-27"><a href="#cb20-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                         <span class="st">"Deveaud2014"</span>)</span>
<span id="cb20-28"><a href="#cb20-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  values<span class="sc">$</span>group <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> base<span class="sc">::</span><span class="fu">factor</span>(values<span class="sc">$</span>group, <span class="at">levels =</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="cn">FALSE</span>,</span>
<span id="cb20-29"><a href="#cb20-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                                        <span class="cn">TRUE</span>), <span class="at">labels =</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="st">"minimize"</span>, <span class="st">"maximize"</span>))</span>
<span id="cb20-30"><a href="#cb20-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  p <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">ggplot</span>(values, <span class="fu">aes_string</span>(<span class="at">x =</span> <span class="st">"topics"</span>, <span class="at">y =</span> <span class="st">"value"</span>,</span>
<span id="cb20-31"><a href="#cb20-31" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                 <span class="at">group =</span> <span class="st">"variable"</span>))</span>

<span id="cb33-4"><a href="#cb33-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>topic_long <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> topic_table[,<span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="dv">2</span><span class="sc">:</span><span class="dv">11</span>)] <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>

<div class="sourceCode cell-code" id="cb40"><pre class="sourceCode r code-with-copy"><code class="sourceCode r"><span id="cb40-1"><a href="#cb40-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>key_df_small<span class="ot">&lt;-</span> key_df</span>

<span id="cb40-30"><a href="#cb40-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">corpus_subset</span>(data_corpus,<span class="sc">!</span>id_numeric <span class="sc">%in%</span> training_id) <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>

<span id="cb40-36"><a href="#cb40-36" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">tokens_remove</span>(<span class="fu">stopwords</span>(<span class="st">"english"</span>, <span class="at">source =</span> <span class="st">"marimo"</span>)) <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>

<span id="cb40-38"><a href="#cb40-38" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">tokens_remove</span>(<span class="fu">stopwords</span>(<span class="st">"ar"</span>, <span class="at">source =</span> <span class="st">"stopwords-iso"</span>)) <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>
<span id="cb40-39"><a href="#cb40-39" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">dfm</span>() <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>
<span id="cb40-40"><a href="#cb40-40" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">dfm_remove</span>(<span class="at">pattern =</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="st">"*.tt"</span>, <span class="st">"*.uk"</span>, <span class="st">"*.com"</span>, <span class="st">"rt"</span>, <span class="st">"#*"</span>, <span class="st">"@*"</span>, <span class="st">".de"</span>)) <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>
<span id="cb40-41"><a href="#cb40-41" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">dfm_trim</span>(<span class="at">max_termfreq =</span> .<span class="dv">99</span>,<span class="at">termfreq_type =</span> <span class="st">"quantile"</span>,<span class="at">verbose =</span> T) <span class="sc">%&gt;%</span></span>
<span id="cb40-42"><a href="#cb40-42" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">dfm_trim</span>(<span class="at">min_termfreq =</span> .<span class="dv">7</span>,<span class="at">termfreq_type =</span> <span class="st">"quantile"</span>,<span class="at">verbose =</span> T)</span>
<span id="cb40-43"><a href="#cb40-43" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-44"><a href="#cb40-44" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-45"><a href="#cb40-45" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># Train Na√Øve Bayes</span></span>
<span id="cb40-46"><a href="#cb40-46" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>model.NB <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">textmodel_nb</span>(dfmat_training, <span class="fu">docvars</span>(dfmat_training, <span class="st">"screen_name"</span>), <span class="at">prior =</span> <span class="st">"docfreq"</span>)</span>
<span id="cb40-47"><a href="#cb40-47" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-48"><a href="#cb40-48" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># The prior indicates an assumed distribution. </span></span>
<span id="cb40-49"><a href="#cb40-49" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># Here we choose how frequently the categories occur in our data.</span></span>
<span id="cb40-50"><a href="#cb40-50" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-51"><a href="#cb40-51" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>dfmat_matched <span class="ot">&lt;-</span></span>
<span id="cb40-52"><a href="#cb40-52" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="fu">dfm_match</span>(dfmat_test, <span class="at">features =</span> <span class="fu">featnames</span>(dfmat_training))</span>
<span id="cb40-53"><a href="#cb40-53" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-54"><a href="#cb40-54" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>actual_class <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">docvars</span>(dfmat_matched, <span class="st">"screen_name"</span>)</span>
<span id="cb40-55"><a href="#cb40-55" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>predicted_class <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">predict</span>(model.NB, <span class="at">newdata =</span> dfmat_matched)</span>
<span id="cb40-56"><a href="#cb40-56" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>tab_class <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">table</span>(actual_class, predicted_class)</span>
<span id="cb40-57"><a href="#cb40-57" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-58"><a href="#cb40-58" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>confusion <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">confusionMatrix</span>(tab_class, <span class="at">mode =</span> <span class="st">"everything"</span>, <span class="at">positive =</span> <span class="st">"genislam1"</span>)</span>

<section id="lasso-and-elastic-net-regularized-generalized-linear-models-glmnet" class="level3">
<h3 class="anchored" data-anchor-id="lasso-and-elastic-net-regularized-generalized-linear-models-glmnet">Lasso and Elastic-Net Regularized Generalized Linear Models (glmnet)</h3>
<div class="cell">
<details>
<summary>Code</summary>
<div class="sourceCode cell-code" id="cb47"><pre class="sourceCode r code-with-copy"><code class="sourceCode r"><span id="cb47-1"><a href="#cb47-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="do">## Fitting a glmnet model with more variables</span></span>
<span id="cb47-2"><a href="#cb47-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">set.seed</span>(<span class="dv">1234</span>)</span>
<span id="cb47-3"><a href="#cb47-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>account_y <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">factor</span>(all_islam<span class="sc">$</span>account, <span class="at">levels =</span> <span class="fu">c</span>(<span class="st">"other"</span>, <span class="st">"genislam"</span>))</span>
<span id="cb47-4"><a href="#cb47-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>account_x <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">select</span>(all_islam, grievance,display_text_width, </span>
<span id="cb47-5"><a href="#cb47-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                    retweet_count, favorite_count)</span>
<span id="cb47-6"><a href="#cb47-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb47-7"><a href="#cb47-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># Create custom indices: myFolds (for a 10-fold CV)</span></span>
<span id="cb47-8"><a href="#cb47-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>myFolds <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">createFolds</span>(account_y, <span class="at">k =</span> <span class="dv">10</span>)</span>
<span id="cb47-9"><a href="#cb47-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb47-10"><a href="#cb47-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># Create reusable trainControl object: myControl</span></span>
<span id="cb47-11"><a href="#cb47-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>myControl <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">trainControl</span>(</span>
<span id="cb47-12"><a href="#cb47-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">summaryFunction =</span> twoClassSummary,</span>
<span id="cb47-13"><a href="#cb47-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">classProbs =</span> <span class="cn">TRUE</span>, <span class="co"># IMPORTANT!</span></span>
<span id="cb47-14"><a href="#cb47-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="at">verboseIter =</span> <span class="cn">TRUE</span>,</span>

<span id="cb47-18"><a href="#cb47-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb47-19"><a href="#cb47-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>train <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">data.frame</span>(account_x, account_y) </span>
<span id="cb47-20"><a href="#cb47-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>

<summary>Code</summary>
<div class="sourceCode cell-code" id="cb57"><pre class="sourceCode r code-with-copy"><code class="sourceCode r"><span id="cb57-1"><a href="#cb57-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"># RF performs best, also outlier folds (see spikes and near zero values)</span></span>
<span id="cb57-2"><a href="#cb57-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>bwtheme <span class="ot">&lt;-</span> <span class="fu">standard.theme</span>(<span class="st">"pdf"</span>, <span class="at">color=</span><span class="cn">FALSE</span>)</span>

<script id="quarto-html-after-body" type="application/javascript">
window.document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function (event) {
  const toggleBodyColorMode = (bsSheetEl) => {
    const mode = bsSheetEl.getAttribute("data-mode");
    const bodyEl = window.document.querySelector("body");
    if (mode === "dark") {
      bodyEl.classList.add("quarto-dark");
      bodyEl.classList.remove("quarto-light");
    } else {
      bodyEl.classList.add("quarto-light");
      bodyEl.classList.remove("quarto-dark");
    }
  }
  const toggleBodyColorPrimary = () => {
    const bsSheetEl = window.document.querySelector("link#quarto-bootstrap");
    if (bsSheetEl) {
      toggleBodyColorMode(bsSheetEl);
    }
  }
  toggleBodyColorPrimary();  
  const icon = "Óßã";
  const anchorJS = new window.AnchorJS();
  anchorJS.options = {
    placement: 'right',
    icon: icon
  };
  anchorJS.add('.anchored');
  const clipboard = new window.ClipboardJS('.code-copy-button', {
    target: function(trigger) {
      return trigger.previousElementSibling;
    }
  });
  clipboard.on('success', function(e) {
    // button target
    const button = e.trigger;
    // don't keep focus
    button.blur();
    // flash "checked"
    button.classList.add('code-copy-button-checked');
    var currentTitle = button.getAttribute("title");
    button.setAttribute("title", "Copied!");
    setTimeout(function() {
      button.setAttribute("title", currentTitle);
      button.classList.remove('code-copy-button-checked');
    }, 1000);
    // clear code selection
    e.clearSelection();
  });
  function tippyHover(el, contentFn) {
    const config = {
      allowHTML: true,
      content: contentFn,
      maxWidth: 500,
      delay: 100,
      arrow: false,
      appendTo: function(el) {
          return el.parentElement;
      },
      interactive: true,
      interactiveBorder: 10,
      theme: 'quarto',
      placement: 'bottom-start'
    };
    window.tippy(el, config); 
  }
  const noterefs = window.document.querySelectorAll('a[role="doc-noteref"]');
  for (var i=0; i<noterefs.length; i++) {
    const ref = noterefs[i];
    tippyHover(ref, function() {
      // use id or data attribute instead here
      let href = ref.getAttribute('data-footnote-href') || ref.getAttribute('href');
      try { href = new URL(href).hash; } catch {}
      const id = href.replace(/^#\/?/, "");
      const note = window.document.getElementById(id);
      return note.innerHTML;
    });
  }
  var bibliorefs = window.document.querySelectorAll('a[role="doc-biblioref"]');
  for (var i=0; i<bibliorefs.length; i++) {
    const ref = bibliorefs[i];
    const cites = ref.parentNode.getAttribute('data-cites').split(' ');
    tippyHover(ref, function() {
      var popup = window.document.createElement('div');
      cites.forEach(function(cite) {
        var citeDiv = window.document.createElement('div');
        citeDiv.classList.add('hanging-indent');
        citeDiv.classList.add('csl-entry');
        var biblioDiv = window.document.getElementById('ref-' + cite);
        if (biblioDiv) {
          citeDiv.innerHTML = biblioDiv.innerHTML;
        }
        popup.appendChild(citeDiv);
      });
      return popup.innerHTML;
    });
  }
});
</script>
